## 🔍 Cross-Page Patterns: Common HTML Issues

These HTML patterns cause the same accessibility errors across multiple pages. **Fix the pattern once in your codebase to fix it everywhere!**

### 🎯 Top Patterns to Fix (Highest Impact)

#### Pattern 1: Affects 75 page(s) - 433 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R74: No description](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r74)
**Issue**: The font size is specified using an absolute unit

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<p>...</p>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/p
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/p')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://texas.gov/
- https://texas.gov/about/site-policies/accessibility-policy/
- https://texas.gov/es/acerca/politicas-del-sitio/politica-de-accesibilidad/
- https://texas.gov/search/
- https://texas.gov/es/search/
- *...and 70 more page(s)*

#### Pattern 3: Affects 75 page(s) - 225 occurrence(s)

**Scanner**: ALFA
**Rule**: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**Issue**: The element does not have a unique ID

**HTML Pattern**:
```html
<g id="Page-1" stroke="none" stroke-width="1" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd">...</g>
```

**XPath** (use in browser DevTools):
```
/g[@id="Page-1"]
```

**How to Replicate**:
1. Open any affected page in your browser
2. Press F12 to open DevTools
3. Go to Console tab
4. Run: `$x('/g[@id="Page-1"]')`
5. The element will be highlighted

**Affected Pages**:
- https://texas.gov/
- https://texas.gov/about/site-policies/accessibility-policy/

## Detailed Failure Information (ALFA)

### https://texas.gov/

#### Rule: [SIA-R111: Interactive elements have a sufficient target size](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r111)
**WCAG**: [SC 2.5.8](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/target-size-minimum) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="main-nav__nav-button" aria-expanded="false" aria-label="Find Services">Find Services</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="main-nav__nav-button"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="main-nav__nav-button" aria-expanded="false" href="/texas-by-texas/">Texas by Texas</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="main-nav__nav-button"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a class="language-switcher__link language-switcher__desktop-link" href="/es/">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="language-switcher__link language-switcher__desktop-link"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<button class="search-icon__container" aria-label="Search">...</button>`
- XPath: `/button[@class="search-icon__container"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: Target has insufficient size
- HTML: `<a href="https://www.youtube.com/playlist?list=PLQxgYir_bwEcaSAxctoYWI__tS1tMbuBf" class="links-helper__external " target="__blank">...</a>`
- XPath: `/a[@class="links-helper__external "]`

*... and 1 more failures for this rule*

#### Rule: [SIA-R3: lang attribute has a valid language code](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r3)
**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID

**WCAG**: [SC 3.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/language-of-page) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<circle id="Oval-2" stroke="#6C7782" stroke-width="2" cx="10.875" cy="10.875" r="7.125" />`

- XPath: `/g[@id="Page-1"]`

- XPath: `/g[@id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services"]`

**Failure 2:**

- HTML: `<path d="M4.05719096,5 L0.528595479,8.52859548 C0.268245951,8.78894501 0.268245951,9.21105499 0.528595479,9.47140452 C0.788945007,9.73175405 1.21105499,9.73175405 1.47140452,9.47140452 L5.47140452,5.47140452 C5.73175405,5.21105499 5.73175405,4.78894501 5.47140452,4.52859548 L1.47140452,0.528595479 C1.21105499,0.268245951 0.788945007,0.268245951 0.528595479,0.528595479 C0.268245951,0.788945007 0.268245951,1.21105499 0.528595479,1.47140452 L4.05719096,5 Z" id="path-1" />`
- XPath: `/path[@id="path-1"]`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="Page-1" stroke="none" stroke-width="1" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="Page-1"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services" transform="translate(-1046.000000, -3780.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="footer-/-temporary-/-desktop" transform="translate(0.000000, 3716.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="footer-/-temporary-/-desktop"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="social-icons" transform="translate(1046.000000, 64.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="social-icons"]`

- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<circle id="Oval-2" stroke="#6C7782" stroke-width="2" cx="10.875" cy="10.875" r="7.125" />`
- XPath: `/circle[@id="Oval-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="Page-1" stroke="none" stroke-width="1" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="Page-1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services" transform="translate(-1046.000000, -3780.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services"]`

**Failure 5:**

- XPath: `/g[@id="footer-/-temporary-/-desktop"]`

- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<circle id="Oval-2" stroke="#6C7782" stroke-width="2" cx="10.875" cy="10.875" r="7.125" />`
- XPath: `/circle[@id="Oval-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="Page-1" stroke="none" stroke-width="1" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="Page-1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services" transform="translate(-1046.000000, -3780.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="footer-/-temporary-/-desktop" transform="translate(0.000000, 3716.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="footer-/-temporary-/-desktop"]`

- HTML: `<p class="service-card__sub-title">Agency: </p>`

- HTML: `<p class="service-card__agency-name">Health Services, Department of State (DSHS)</p>`

- HTML: `<p class="footer__copyright">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="footer__copyright"]`

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The highest possible contrast of the text is 5.17:1 which is         below the required contrast of 7:1

- HTML: `<p>Directorio de servicios gubernamentales  Texas  of...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

- HTML: `<g id="Page-1" stroke="none" stroke-width="1" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd">...</g>`

**WCAG**: [SC 1.1.1](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/non-text-content) (Level A)

**Failure 1:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p>...</p>`
- XPath: `/p`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: The line height is specified using an absolute unit
- HTML: `<p class="agency-card__sub-title">Dirección</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="agency-card__sub-title"]`

**Failure 3:**

- HTML: `<p class="footer__copyright">...</p>`
- XPath: `/p[@class="footer__copyright"]`

- XPath: `/circle[@id="Oval-2"]`

**Failure 3:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="Page-1" stroke="none" stroke-width="1" fill="none" fill-rule="evenodd">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="Page-1"]`

**Failure 4:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services" transform="translate(-1046.000000, -3780.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="2.0-Main-Landing_Driver-Services"]`

**Failure 5:**
- Message: The element does not have a unique ID
- HTML: `<g id="footer-/-temporary-/-desktop" transform="translate(0.000000, 3716.000000)">...</g>`
- XPath: `/g[@id="footer-/-temporary-/-desktop"]`

#### Rule: [SIA-R73: Text spacing can be adjusted without loss of content](https://alfa.siteimprove.com/rules/sia-r73)
**WCAG**: [SC 1.4.12](https://www.w3.org/WAI/WCAG22/Understanding/text-spacing) (Level AA)

**Failure 1:**

- HTML: `<p>...</p>`

- XPath: `/p[@class="w-2/3 post__description-optional mt-0 mb-0"]`

## Detailed Failure Information (axe)

### https://texas.gov/

#### Rule: [heading-order](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/heading-order?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: Heading levels should only increase by one
- HTML: `<h4>About Us</h4>`
- XPath: `.footer__list:nth-child(1) > h4`

#### Rule: [region](https://dequeuniversity.com/rules/axe/4.11/region?application=playwright)
**Impact**: moderate

**Failure 1:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div data-testid="alert" class="alert-banner alert-banner__type-2">`
- XPath: `.alert-banner`

**Failure 2:**
- Message: All page content should be contained by landmarks
- HTML: `<div class="cookies-banner__description"><p>The site uses cookies to provide you with a great user experience. By using Texas.gov, you accept our use of cookies. For more detail, view our Site Policies.</p></div>`
- XPath: `.cookies-banner__description`

- XPath: `.cookies-banner__description`

- HTML: `<div class="cookies-banner__description"><p>The site uses cookies to provide you with a great user experience. By using Texas.gov, you accept our use of cookies. For more detail, view our Site Policies.</p></div>`
- XPath: `.cookies-banner__description`
